GSR Usage
---------

GSR Component:
   The local reset signal 'counter_0_countDone' of the design has been inferred
        as Global Set Reset (GSR). The reset signal used for GSR control is
        'counter_0_countDone'.
        

     GSR Property:
   The design components with GSR property set to ENABLED will respond to global
        set reset while the components with GSR property set to DISABLED will
        not.
        

     Components on inferred reset domain with GSR Property disabled
--------------------------------------------------------------

     These components have the GSR property set to DISABLED and are on the
     inferred reset domain. The components will respond to the reset signal
     'counter_0_countDone' via the local reset on the component and not the GSR
     component.

     Type and number of components of the type: 
   Register = 13 

     Type and instance name of component: 
   Register : packetGen_1/current_state_FSM_i1
   Register : packetGen_1/symCounter__i0
   Register : packetGen_1/symVal_43
   Register : packetGen_1/symCounter__i7
   Register : packetGen_1/symCounter__i6
   Register : packetGen_1/symCounter__i5
   Register : packetGen_1/symCounter__i4
   Register : packetGen_1/symCounter__i3
   Register : packetGen_1/symCounter__i2
   Register : packetGen_1/symCounter__i1
   Register : packetGen_1/current_state_FSM_i4
   Register : packetGen_1/current_state_FSM_i3
   Register : packetGen_1/current_state_FSM_i2


     Components with synchronous local reset also reset by asynchronous GSR
----------------------------------------------------------------------

     These components have the GSR property set to ENABLED and the local reset
     is synchronous. The components will respond to the synchronous local reset
     and to the unrelated asynchronous reset signal 'counter_0_countDone' via
     the GSR component.

     Type and number of components of the type: 
   ALU54B = 42, MULT18X18D = 84
